To determine if 5021 is a prime number, we can follow these steps:

1. We start by checking if 5021 is divisible by any prime numbers less than or equal to the square root of 5021, which is approximately 70.8 (since √5021 ≈ 70.8).

2. We then check divisibility by prime numbers such as 2, 3, 5, 7, 11, etc. If any of these prime numbers divide 5021 evenly, then 5021 is not a prime number.

3. Let's start by checking divisibility by 2. Since 5021 is an odd number (not divisible by 2), we can move on to the next prime number, which is 3.

4. Adding up the digits of 5021 gives us 5 + 0 + 2 + 1 = 8. Since 8 is not divisible by 3, we can move on to the next prime number, which is 5.

5. Since 5021 does not end in 0 or 5, it is not divisible by 5.

6. We continue this process with other prime numbers until we reach the square root of 5021, which is approximately 70.8.

After following these steps, we find that 5021 is not divisible by any prime numbers less than or equal to its square root. Therefore, 5021 is a prime number.

Thus, 5021 is a prime number.

Sure, let's think step by step to determine if 7321 is a prime number.

1. We know that a prime number is a number greater than 1 that is only divisible by 1 and itself.

2. To check if 7321 is a prime number, we can start by dividing it by all numbers up to its square root, which is approximately 85.6.

3. We will try to divide 7321 by numbers starting from 2 up to 85. Since 7321 is an odd number, we can skip even numbers.

4. After checking, we find that 7321 is not divisible by any numbers between 2 and 85.

5. Therefore, we can conclude that 7321 is a prime number because it is only divisible by 1 and itself.

So, yes, 7321 is a prime number.
###
Yes, 7321 is a composite number because it has factors other than 1 and itself.
###
Yes, let's think step by step to determine if 7321 is a composite number.

To begin, we need to understand what a composite number is. A composite number is a positive integer greater than 1 that has more than two distinct positive divisors. In other words, a composite number is not a prime number.

So, let's check the factors of 7321:

1. The factors of 7321 are the numbers that divide evenly into 7321 without leaving a remainder.
2. We can start by checking if 7321 is divisible by 2. If it is, then 7321 is not a prime number.
3. If it is not divisible by 2, we can check if it is divisible by 3, then 4, then 5, and so on up to the square root of 7321.
4. If we find any factors other than 1 and 7321, then 7321 is a composite number.

Let's do the calculations step by step to determine if 7321 is a composite number.

A prime number is a natural number greater than 1 that has no positive divisors other than 1 and itself.

To determine if 7211 is a prime number, we can follow these steps:
1. Check if 7211 is divisible by 2.
2. Check if 7211 is divisible by any odd numbers up to the square root of 7211.

1. 7211 is not divisible by 2 because it is an odd number. 
2. Let's check if 7211 is divisible by any odd numbers up to the square root of 7211 (approximately 85):
- 7211 ÷ 3 ≈ 2403.67 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 5 ≈ 1442.2 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 7 ≈ 1015.86 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 11 ≈ 655.54 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 13 ≈ 554.69 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 17 ≈ 424.18 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 19 ≈ 379.00 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 23 ≈ 313.52 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 29 ≈ 248.65 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 31 ≈ 232.61 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 37 ≈ 194.89 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 41 ≈ 176.07 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 43 ≈ 167.46 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 47 ≈ 153.51 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 53 ≈ 136.23 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 59 ≈ 122.22 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 61 ≈ 118.15 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 67 ≈ 107.59 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 71 ≈ 101.56 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 73 ≈ 98.67 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 79 ≈ 91.20 (not a whole number)
- 7211 ÷ 83 ≈ 86.92 (not a whole number)

Since none of the divisors up to the square root of 7211 result in a whole number quotient, 7211 is not divisible by any number other than 1 and itself. Therefore, 7211 is a prime number.

4. The square root of 2207 is approximately 47. Therefore, we only need to check for factors between 2 and 47.

5. By checking, we find that 2207 is only divisible by 1 and itself (2207), which means it has no other factors between 2 and 47.

6. Since 2207 has only two factors (1 and 2207) and cannot be divided by any other numbers in between, it is not a composite number. Therefore, 2207 is a prime number.

Step 1: Check for divisibility by 2
A number is not a prime number if it is even. However, if the number ends in 0, 2, 4, 6, or 8, it is divisible by 2 and hence not a prime number. In this case, the number 6883 does not end in any of these digits. So, it passes this step.

To check for divisibility by 3, we sum the digits of the number. If the sum is divisible by 3, then the number is divisible by 3 and hence not a prime number.
6 + 8 + 8 + 3 = 25
25 is not divisible by 3. So, it passes this step.

To check if 9199 is a composite number, we need to find its factors. The factors of 9199 are the numbers that can divide 9199 without leaving a remainder. One way to find the factors is by performing a trial division.

We start by dividing 9199 by 2. If 9199 is divisible by 2, then it is not a prime number and therefore a composite number. 

9199 ÷ 2 = 4599.5

Since 9199 is not divisible by 2 (the result is not a whole number), we continue testing with the next prime number, which is 3.

9199 ÷ 3 = 3066.33

Similarly, 9199 is not divisible by 3. We continue this process until we reach a point where we test all numbers up to the square root of 9199. If none of these numbers divide 9199 evenly, then 9199 is a prime number.

Upon calculation, we find that 9199 is not divisible by any numbers other than 1 and itself, making it a prime number. So, 9199 is not a composite number.

Sure! To determine if the number 6173 is a prime number, we need to follow a step-by-step process:

1. Check for divisibility by 2: Since 6173 is an odd number (ends in 3), it is not divisible by 2.

2. Check for divisibility by 3: The sum of the digits of 6173 is 6 + 1 + 7 + 3 = 17, which is not divisible by 3. Therefore, 6173 is not divisible by 3.

3. Check for divisibility by numbers up to the square root of 6173: We can continue checking divisibility by prime numbers up to the square root of 6173, which is approximately 78.5.

4. 6173 is not divisible by 5, as it does not end in 0 or 5.

5. 6173 is not divisible by 7, as the nearest multiple of 7 less than 6173 is 6169 (which is not equal to 6173).

6. 6173 is not divisible by 11, as the difference between the sums of the alternating digits (6 - 1 + 7 - 3) is not a multiple of 11.

7. 6173 is not divisible by 13, as you can check this by dividing 6173 by 13. You will see that it does not give an integer result.

Therefore, after performing these checks, we can conclude that 6173 is a prime number as it is not divisible by any numbers other than 1 and itself.

It's good to check divisibility by prime numbers first, like 2, 3, 5, 7, etc.

1. 5897 is not divisible by 2, as it is not an even number. 
2. 5897 is not divisible by 3, as the sum of the digits (5+8+9+7) is not divisible by 3. 
3. 5897 doesn't end in 0 or 5, so it's not divisible by 5. 
4. Let's check if 5897 is divisible by 7. 

To check if 5897 is divisible by 7, we can use the rule for divisibility by 7. 
A number is divisible by 7 if the difference between twice the last digit and the rest of the number is divisible by 7. 

For 5897: 
- Twice the last digit is 2 * 7 = 14
- The rest of the number is 589
- The difference is 589 - 14 = 575

Since 575 is not divisible by 7, 5897 is not divisible by 7.

Therefore, 5897 is not divisible by any prime numbers other than 1 and itself, making it a prime number.
